local masteryParagraph = nil
local masteryToggle = nil

local function updateParagraph(text)
    if masteryParagraph then
        pcall(function()
            masteryParagraph:Set(text)
        end)
    end
end

local GloveMasteryClient
task.spawn(function()
    local deps = game:GetService("ReplicatedFirst"):FindFirstChild("Dependencies")
    if deps then
        local mod = deps:FindFirstChild("GloveMasteryClient")
        if mod then
            pcall(function() 
                GloveMasteryClient = require(mod) 
            end)
        end
    end
end)

local GLOVE_ALIASES = {
    ["Moai"] = "🗿",
    ["moai"] = "🗿",
    ["Moyai"] = "🗿"
}

local function getActiveGlove()
    local target = nil
    
    local ls = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
    if ls and ls:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
        local glove = ls.Glove.Value
        if glove and glove ~= "" and glove ~= "None" then
            target = glove
        end
    end
    
    if not target and player.Character then
        local tool = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
        if tool and tool.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
            target = tool.Name
        end
    end
    
    if not target then
        local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
        if backpack then
            local tool = backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
            if tool then
                target = tool.Name
            end
        end
    end

    if target and GLOVE_ALIASES[target] then
        return GLOVE_ALIASES[target], target
    end
    
    return target, target
end

local function isQuestCompleted(taskInfo)
    if taskInfo.Completed ~= nil then
        return taskInfo.Completed == true
    end
    
    local currentValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressCurrent) or 0
    local maxValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressMax) or 1
    
    return currentValue >= maxValue
end

local lastRenderedKey = ""

local function renderOverlay(rows, currentGloveDisplay)
    local keyParts = { tostring(currentGloveDisplay or "Mastery") }
    for _, row in ipairs(rows) do
        table.insert(keyParts, tostring(row.quest) .. "|" .. tostring(row.progress) .. "|" .. tostring(row.completed))
    end

    local newKey = table.concat(keyParts, ";")
    if newKey == lastRenderedKey then return end
    lastRenderedKey = newKey

    for _, child in ipairs(contentFrame:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("TextLabel") then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end

    local displayName = tostring(currentGloveDisplay or "Mastery")
    titleLabel.Text = displayName

    local count = #rows
    if count == 0 then
        frame.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(340, 32)
        updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. displayName .. "\nNo active quests found.")
        return
    end

    local paragraphLines = {}
    table.insert(paragraphLines, "Glove Mastery: " .. displayName)
    
    for index, row in ipairs(rows) do
        local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        label.Name = "QuestRow"
        label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 44)
        label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, (index - 1) * 44)
        label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        
        local progressText = row.progress or ""
        local completedText = row.completed and " ✅" or ""
        label.Text = tostring(row.quest or "") .. "\n" .. progressText .. completedText
        
        label.TextColor3 = row.completed and Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        label.TextSize = 14
        label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        label.TextWrapped = true
        label.Parent = contentFrame
        
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "")
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "                    QUEST " .. index)
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "")
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "Description: " .. tostring(row.quest or ""))
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "Progress: " .. progressText .. (row.completed and " ✅" or ""))
    end

    frame.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(340, math.clamp(32 + count * 44, 60, 400))
    
    updateParagraph(table.concat(paragraphLines, "\n"))
end

local function renderStatus(title, message)
    if message == "" then
        renderOverlay({}, title or "Mastery")
        updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. tostring(title or "Mastery") .. "\nNo data available.")
    else
        renderOverlay({ { quest = tostring(message or ""), progress = "", completed = false } }, title or "Mastery")
        updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. tostring(title or "Mastery") .. "\n" .. tostring(message))
    end
end

local getthreadidentity = getthreadidentity or getthreadcontext or getidentity or function() return nil end
local setthreadidentity = setthreadidentity or setthreadcontext or setidentity or function() end

task.spawn(function()
    while isTrackerActive do
        task.wait()
        
        local internalGloveName, displayGloveName = getActiveGlove()
        
        if not internalGloveName then
            renderStatus("Mastery", "")
            continue
        end

        if not GloveMasteryClient then
            renderStatus("Mastery", "Loading data...")
            continue
        end

        local originalId = getthreadidentity()
        
        local s, parsedData = pcall(function()
            return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(GloveMasteryClient, internalGloveName)
        end)
        
        if not s then
            s, parsedData = pcall(function()
                return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(internalGloveName)
            end)
        end
        
        if not s and displayGloveName ~= internalGloveName then
            s, parsedData = pcall(function()
                return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(displayGloveName)
            end)
        end

        if originalId then pcall(function() setthreadidentity(originalId) end) end

        if not s or type(parsedData) ~= "table" then
            renderOverlay({}, displayGloveName)
            continue
        end

        local rows = {}
        for _, taskInfo in ipairs(parsedData) do
            local taskName = taskInfo.Name or "Unknown Quest"
            local currentValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressCurrent) or 0
            local maxValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressMax) or 1
            local completed = isQuestCompleted(taskInfo)
            local percent = math.floor((currentValue / maxValue) * 100)
            
            local progressText = tostring(currentValue) .. " / " .. tostring(maxValue) .. " (" .. tostring(percent) .. "%)"
            
            table.insert(rows, {
                quest = taskName,
                progress = progressText,
                completed = completed
            })
        end

        renderOverlay(rows, displayGloveName)
    end
end)

masteryParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph({
    Title = "Glove Mastery Progress:",
    Content = "Loading..."
})

hudGui.Enabled = false
frame.Visible = false

end

local masteryNames = {
    "spin", "Stick", "Brick", "Flash", "Spring", "Dice", "Thanos", "Fort", "Space", "Hive", "Mace", "Killstreak", "Gummy",
    "Engineer", "Phantom", "Wormhole", "Stalker", "Cherry", "Booster", "BONK", "Cloud", "Soul", 
    "[REDACTED]", "bus", "Phase", "Bomb", "Bubble", "Shard", "Moon", "Rage", "Chain", "Tycoon", 
    "🗿", "Obby", "Voodoo", "rob", "Tinkerer", "Glovel", "Firework", "Run", "Frostbite", "Plank", "Hexa", "Eggler", "Car Keys", 
    "Ultra Instinct", "Acrobat"
}

local selectedMastery = masteryNames[1]
local hookfunctionSupported = pcall(function() return hookfunction end)

Tab:AddDropdown("SelectGloveMastery", {
    Title = "Select Glove for Mastery",
    Values = masteryNames,
    Default = 1,
    Callback = function(Value)
        selectedMastery = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Apply Mastery",
    Callback = function()
        if not hookfunctionSupported then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Your executor doesn't support hookfunction",
                Duration = 5
            })
            return
        end
        
        local success, err = pcall(function()
            local mod = require(game.ReplicatedFirst.Dependencies.GloveMasteryClient)
            local old = mod.IsMasteredVersionEnabled
            hookfunction(mod.IsMasteredVersionEnabled, function(self, g)
                return g == selectedMastery or old(self, g)
            end)
        end)
        
        if success then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = selectedMastery .. " mastery applied!",
                Duration = 2
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Failed to apply mastery: " .. tostring(err),
                Duration = 3
            })
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Warning",
                Content = "Your executor doesn't support hookfunction",
                Duration = 5
            })
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Anchor Yourself",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        anchorEnabled = Value
        if Value then
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
                if head then
                    head.Anchored = true
                end
            end
        else
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
                if head then
                    head.Anchored = false
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

local autoDieOnRagdoll = false
Tab:AddToggle("AutoDieRagdoll", {
    Title = "Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoDieOnRagdoll = Value
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoDieOnRagdoll do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Health = 0
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        if safespot then
            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
            if base then
                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                if char then
                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                    end
                end
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Create Safespot first!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local autoSafespot = false
local safespotLoop = nil
Tab:AddToggle("AutoSafespot", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoSafespot = Value
        if Value then
            if safespotLoop then
                task.cancel(safespotLoop)
                safespotLoop = nil
            end
            safespotLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoSafespot do
                    pcall(function()
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                                if char then
                                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if hrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        else
            if safespotLoop then
                task.cancel(safespotLoop)
                safespotLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Create Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        if workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot") == nil then
            local Safespot = Instance.new("Model", workspace)
            Safespot.Name = "Safespot"

            local base = Instance.new("Part")
            base.Name = "Base"
            base.Size = Vector3.new(500, 10, 500)
            base.Position = Vector3.new(10000, -50, 10000)
            base.Anchored = true
            base.CanCollide = true
            base.Transparency = 0.5
            base.Parent = Safespot

            local partsData = {
                {"DefendPart",  Vector3.new(500, 117, 5),   Vector3.new(10000.2, 13, 9752.45)},
                {"DefendPart1", Vector3.new(5, 117, 496),   Vector3.new(10248.2, 13, 10002.4)},
                {"DefendPart2", Vector3.new(497, 117, 6),   Vector3.new(9998.13, 13, 10247.2)},
                {"DefendPart3", Vector3.new(7, 117, 490),   Vector3.new(9752.71, 13, 9999.28)},
                {"DefendPart4", Vector3.new(491, 10, 491),  Vector3.new(10001.1, 76, 9999.66)},
            }

            for _, partInfo in pairs(partsData) do
                local part = Instance.new("Part")
                part.Name = partInfo[1]
                part.Size = partInfo[2]
                part.Position = partInfo[3]
                part.Anchored = true
                part.CanCollide = true
                part.Transparency = 0.5
                part.Parent = Safespot
            end
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = "Safespot Created Successfully!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Safespot already exists!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Misc Stuff")

local antiAfkEnabled = false
Tab:AddToggle("AntiAFK", {
    Title = "Anti AFK",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        antiAfkEnabled = Value
        if Value then
            LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
            end)
        end
    end
})

_G.AntiRagdoll = false
Tab:AddToggle("AntiRagdoll", {
    Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value
        
        if _G.AntiRagdoll then
            task.spawn(function()
                local lastCFrame = nil
                local lastPosition = nil
                local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                local humanoidRootPart = nil
                
                while _G.AntiRagdoll do
                    pcall(function()
                        character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if not character then 
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local ragdolledValue = character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        
                        if humanoidRootPart and (not ragdolledValue or ragdolledValue.Value == false) then
                            lastCFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            lastPosition = humanoidRootPart.Position
                        end
                        
                        if ragdolledValue and ragdolledValue.Value == true and lastCFrame and humanoidRootPart then
                            humanoidRootPart.CFrame = lastCFrame
                            humanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                            humanoidRootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                            
                            for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and part ~= humanoidRootPart then
                                    part.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                    part.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                end
                            end
                            
                            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                                humanoid.Sit = false
                            end
                            
                            task.wait()
                            if character and character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
                                character.Ragdolled.Value = false
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait()
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
                Content = "Enabled! Instant ragdoll prevention.",
                Duration = 2
            })
        end
    end    
})

end

                loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Scripter-Coder/Scripter-Coder/refs/heads/main/Slap%20Battles/Slap%20Battles%20Hub%20OP%20Script%20(Fluent)/Christmas%20Hub.txt"))()
            end
        })

        Tab:AddParagraph({
            Title = "Universal Scripts",
            Content = ""
        })

        Tab:AddButton({
            Title = "Load Infinite Yield",
            Callback = function()
                loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/EdgeIY/infiniteyield/master/source"))()
            end
        })

        Tab:AddButton({

                loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/infyiff/backup/main/dex.lua"))()
            end
        })

        Tab:AddButton({
            Title = "Load Remote Spy",
            Callback = function()
                loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/infyiff/backup/main/SimpleSpyV3/main.lua"))()
            end
        })

-- ============================================================
-- SPIN TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "spin",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character
        
        local hasSpinGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "spin"
        local hasEntered = character and character:FindFirstChild("entered")
        local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        
        if not hasSpinGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
            local errorMsg = ""
            if not hasSpinGlove then
                errorMsg = "Equip Spin Glove"
            elseif not hasEntered then
                errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
            elseif not hasSafespot then
                errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
            end
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = errorMsg,
                Duration = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        if safespot then
            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
            if base then
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                    
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Teleported",
                        Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                        Duration = 2
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- STICK TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Stick",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoStickSafespot = false
local stickSafespotLoop = nil
local stickSlapAuraConnection = nil

Tab:AddToggle("StickReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoStickSafespot = Value
        
        if Value then
            if stickSafespotLoop then
                task.cancel(stickSafespotLoop)
                stickSafespotLoop = nil
            end
            
            stickSafespotLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoStickSafespot do
                    pcall(function()
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                if char then
                                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if hrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            if stickSlapAuraConnection then
                stickSlapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                stickSlapAuraConnection = nil
            end
            
            stickSlapAuraConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not autoStickSafespot then return end
                
                pcall(function()
                    local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                    if not generalHit then return end
                    
                    for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                        if player.Character then
                            local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or 
                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if targetPart then
                                generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Safespot + Slap Aura",
                Content = "Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if stickSafespotLoop then
                task.cancel(stickSafespotLoop)
                stickSafespotLoop = nil
            end
            
            if stickSlapAuraConnection then
                stickSlapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                stickSlapAuraConnection = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoStickReceiver = false
local stickReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("StickHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot (Receiver)",
    Default = false,

        autoStickReceiver = Value

            if not safespot then

                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoStickReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if stickReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(stickReceiverLoop)
                stickReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            stickReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()

                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Teleport",
                Content = "Auto teleport to Safespot (Receiver) enabled!",
                Duration = 2
            })
            
        else
            if stickReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(stickReceiverLoop)
                stickReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Brick",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

local brickMasterRunning = false
local brickMasterConnection = nil
local brickMasterLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("BrickMaster", {
    Title = "Auto Obtain Brick Master Badge",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            local hasBrickGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Brick"
            local hasEntered = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered")
            local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            
            if not hasBrickGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
                local errorMsg = ""
                if not hasBrickGlove then
                    errorMsg = "Equip Brick Glove"
                elseif not hasEntered then
                    errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
                elseif not hasSafespot then
                    errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
                end
                
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if safespot then
                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                if base then
                    local hrp = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                    end
                end
            end
            
            task.wait(0.5)
            
            getgenv().BrickMasterLoop = true
            brickMasterLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().BrickMasterLoop do
                    pcall(function()
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                if char then
                                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if hrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local lbrick = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("lbrick")
                        if lbrick then
                            lbrick:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        pcall(function()
                            local gui = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("BRICKCOUNT")
                            if gui then
                                local imageLabel = gui:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
                                if imageLabel then
                                    local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                                    if textLabel then
                                        local currentCount = tonumber(textLabel.Text) or 0
                                        textLabel.Text = tostring(currentCount + 1)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end)
                    task.wait(1.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Brick Master",
                Content = "Auto Obtain Brick Master Badge Started!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            getgenv().BrickMasterLoop = false
            if brickMasterLoop then
                task.cancel(brickMasterLoop)
                brickMasterLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end    
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoBrickHelper = false
local brickHelperLoop = nil
local TARGET_UNION_SIZE = Vector3.new(1.3293739557266235, 0.4905083179473877, 0.8358331918716431)

Tab:AddToggle("BrickHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Teleport To Bricks",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoBrickHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoBrickHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if brickHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(brickHelperLoop)
                brickHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            brickHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoBrickHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local targetPart = nil
                                for _, part in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if part:IsA("Part") and part.Name == "Union" then
                                        if part.Size.X == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.X and 
                                           part.Size.Y == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Y and 
                                           part.Size.Z == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Z then
                                            targetPart = part
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                if targetPart then
                                    hrp.CFrame = targetPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Teleport",
                Content = "Auto teleport to Safespot/Bricks enabled!",
                Duration = 2
            })
            
        else
            if brickHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(brickHelperLoop)
                brickHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("3 Quest")

Tab:AddToggle("BrickFling", {
    Title = "Auto Fling Bricks",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Brick" then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Brick Glove first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            local TARGET_UNION_SIZE = Vector3.new(1.3293739557266235, 0.4905083179473877, 0.8358331918716431)
            
            getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = true
            
            task.spawn(function()
                local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
                local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local flinging = true
                
                local noclipConnection
                noclipConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                    if speaker.Character then
                        for _, part in pairs(speaker.Character:GetDescendants()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.CanCollide then
                                part.CanCollide = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                local function onCharacterAdded(char)
                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                    if humanoid then
                        humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                            flinging = false
                            if noclipConnection then
                                noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                            end
                            getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                local humanoid = speaker.Character and speaker.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                        flinging = false
                        if noclipConnection then
                            noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                        end
                        getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
                    end)
                end
                
                speaker.CharacterAdded:Connect(onCharacterAdded)
                
                while getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop and flinging do
                    RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                    local character = speaker.Character
                    local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    local vel, movel = nil, 0.1

                    while not (character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent) do
                        RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                        character = speaker.Character
                        root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    end

                    vel = root.Velocity
                    root.Velocity = vel * 10000 + Vector3.new(0, 10000, 0)

                    RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
                    if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
                        root.Velocity = vel
                    end

                    RunService.Stepped:Wait()
                    if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
                        root.Velocity = vel + Vector3.new(0, movel, 0)
                        movel = movel * -1
                    end
                    
                    for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Name == "Union" then
                            if obj.Size.X == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.X and 
                               obj.Size.Y == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Y and 
                               obj.Size.Z == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Z then
                                pcall(function()
                                    local originalCFrame = obj.CFrame
                                    local originalAnchored = obj.Anchored
                                    
                                    obj.Anchored = false
                                    obj.CFrame = root.CFrame
                                    task.wait(0.01)
                                    
                                    obj.CFrame = originalCFrame
                                    obj.Anchored = originalAnchored
                                end)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    
                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
                
                if noclipConnection then
                    noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Fling Bricks",
                Content = "Enabled! Flinging and bringing Unions.",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
        end
    end    
})

end

            for i = 1, 1500 do
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("FlashTeleport"):FireServer()
                task.wait()
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({

            })
        end
    end

    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoFlashReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoFlashReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if flashReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(flashReceiverLoop)
                flashReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            flashReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()

                    pcall(function()

                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        if flashTeleport then
                            flashTeleport:FireServer()

                        task.wait(3)

                        if flashHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        flashHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })

            if flashReceiverLoop then

            end

-- SPRING TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Spring",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoSpringReceiver = false
local springReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("SpringReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Jump + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoSpringReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoSpringReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if springReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(springReceiverLoop)
                springReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            springReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoSpringReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                            
                            if hrp and humanoid then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(9999, -42, 9991)
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                
                                humanoid.JumpPower = 1
                                task.wait(0.05)
                                
                                humanoid.Jump = true
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                local springhit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("springhit")
                                if springhit then
                                    local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                    for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                        if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                            local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                              player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                            if targetPart then
                                                springhit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Jump + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if springReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(springReceiverLoop)
                springReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            pcall(function()
                local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if char then
                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    if humanoid then
                        humanoid.JumpPower = 50
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Dice",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoDiceReceiver = false
local diceReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("DiceReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoDiceReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoDiceReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if diceReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(diceReceiverLoop)
                diceReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            diceReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoDiceReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local diceHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("DiceHit")
                        if diceHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        diceHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if diceReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(diceReceiverLoop)
                diceReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoDiceHelper = false
local diceHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("DiceHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Enter Arena + Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoDiceHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoDiceHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if diceHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(diceHelperLoop)
                diceHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            diceHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoDiceHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        local dicePart = workspace:FindFirstChild("DicePart")
                        
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                        end
                        
                        if dicePart then
                            local billboard = dicePart:FindFirstChild("BillboardGui")
                            if billboard then
                                local imageLabel = billboard:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
                                if imageLabel then
                                    local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                                    if textLabel then
                                        local text = textLabel.Text
                                        local number = tonumber(text)
                                        if number and number >= 60 then
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Enter Arena + Teleport + Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if diceHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(diceHelperLoop)
                diceHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Thanos",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoThanosReceiver = false
local thanosReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("ThanosReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoThanosReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoThanosReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if thanosReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(thanosReceiverLoop)
                thanosReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            thanosReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local abilityTimer = 0
                
                while autoThanosReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                        if abilityTimer >= 3 then
                            abilityTimer = 0
                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer(2)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura + Ability Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if thanosReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(thanosReceiverLoop)
                thanosReceiverLoop = nil

-- ============================================================
-- FORT TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Fort",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Badge + Plank Glove",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Fort" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            local hrp = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            local originalPos = hrp.CFrame

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 97, 4)
            wait(0.2)
            hrp.Anchored = true
            wait(0.3)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Fortlol:FireServer()
            wait(3.5)
            hrp.Anchored = false
            wait(0.1)
            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 106, -6)
            wait(0.5)
            hrp.CFrame = originalPos
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Fort Glove/Enter Arena",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2-3 Quest")

local autoFortDestroy = false
local fortDestroyLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("FortDestroy", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Destroy Fort Walls",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoFortDestroy = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoFortDestroy = false
                return
            end
            
            if fortDestroyLoop then
                task.cancel(fortDestroyLoop)
                fortDestroyLoop = nil
            end
            
            fortDestroyLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoFortDestroy do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local fortlol = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Fortlol")
                        if fortlol then
                            fortlol:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local targetPart = nil
                        local targetColor = Color3.fromRGB(172, 73, 73)
                        
                        for _, part in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name == "Part" then
                                local partColor = part.Color
                                if partColor.R == targetColor.R and 
                                   partColor.G == targetColor.G and 
                                   partColor.B == targetColor.B then
                                    targetPart = part
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        if targetPart then
                            hrp.CFrame = targetPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            
                            task.wait(0.3)
                            
                            local selfKnockback = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("SelfKnockback")
                            if selfKnockback then
                                selfKnockback:FireServer({ 
                                    Force = 0, 
                                    Direction = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0) 
                                })
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    task.wait(4)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Fort Destroy",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Destroy Fort Walls Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if fortDestroyLoop then
                task.cancel(fortDestroyLoop)
                fortDestroyLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- SPACE TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Space",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

Tab:AddToggle("SpaceAbility", {
    Title = "Auto Use Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Space" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                getgenv().SpaceAbilityLoop = true
                task.spawn(function()
                    while getgenv().SpaceAbilityLoop do
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ZeroGSound:FireServer()
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Space Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
        else
            getgenv().SpaceAbilityLoop = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using bus?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "bus" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the bus glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the bus glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To bus Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "bus" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "bus Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle("SpaceBus", {
    Title = "Auto Bring Bus",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value) 
        Giftfarm = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while Giftfarm do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.01) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "BusModel" and v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                        pcall(function()
                            local originalCFrame = v.CFrame
                            local originalAnchored = v.Anchored
                            
                            for _, child in pairs(v:GetChildren()) do
                                if child:IsA("TouchInterest") then
                                    child:Destroy()
                                end
                            end
                            
                            v.Anchored = false
                            v.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 0, 5)
                            task.wait(0.05)
                        end)
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.05)
            end
        end)
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Space Glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

            spaceHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoSpaceHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                Duration = 2
            })
            
        else
            if spaceHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(spaceHelperLoop)
                spaceHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end

})

Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoHiveReceiver = false
local hiveReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("HiveReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHiveReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoHiveReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if hiveReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(hiveReceiverLoop)
                hiveReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            hiveReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHiveReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if hiveReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(hiveReceiverLoop)
                hiveReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end

})

Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoMaceReceiver = false
local maceReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("MaceReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoMaceReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoMaceReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if maceReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(maceReceiverLoop)
                maceReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            maceReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoMaceReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
