                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart, 93.05674743652344)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if maceReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(maceReceiverLoop)
                maceReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoMaceHelper = false
local maceHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("MaceHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoMaceHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoMaceHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if maceHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(maceHelperLoop)
                maceHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            maceHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoMaceHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if maceHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(maceHelperLoop)
                maceHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoEngineerReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if engineerReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(engineerReceiverLoop)
                engineerReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            engineerReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local abilityTimer = 0
                
                while autoEngineerReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                        if abilityTimer >= 6 then
                            abilityTimer = 0
                            local sentry = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Sentry")
                            if sentry then
                                sentry:FireServer()
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Sentry Ability Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if engineerReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(engineerReceiverLoop)
                engineerReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoEngineerHelper = false
local engineerHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("EngineerHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver/Sentry's Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoEngineerHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoEngineerHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if engineerHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(engineerHelperLoop)
                engineerHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            engineerHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoEngineerHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local turret = workspace:FindFirstChild("Turret")
                        if turret then
                            local hingePart = turret:FindFirstChild("HingePart")
                            if hingePart then
                                local glove = hingePart:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                if glove then
                                    hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if engineerHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(engineerHelperLoop)
                engineerHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- PHANTOM TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Phantom",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoPhantomReceiver = false
local phantomReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("PhantomReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoPhantomReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoPhantomReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if phantomReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(phantomReceiverLoop)
                phantomReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            phantomReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoPhantomReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local phantomDash = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhantomDash")
                        if phantomDash then
                            local phantom = char and char:FindFirstChild("Phantom")
                            if phantom then
                                phantomDash:InvokeServer(phantom)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.01)
                        
                        local phantomHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhantomHit")
                        if phantomHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        phantomHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Phantom Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if phantomReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(phantomReceiverLoop)
                phantomReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

-- ============================================================
-- WORMHOLE TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Wormhole",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoWormholeReceiver = false
local wormholeReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("WormholeReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura + Auto Teleport To Circle Portals",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoWormholeReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoWormholeReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if wormholeReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(wormholeReceiverLoop)
                wormholeReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            wormholeReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local portalTimer = 0
                
                while autoWormholeReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local wormholePlace = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormholePlace")
                        if wormholePlace then
                            wormholePlace:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local wormHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormHit")
                        if wormHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        wormHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        portalTimer = portalTimer + 0.5
                        if portalTimer >= 2 then
                            portalTimer = 0
                            
                            local wormholes = workspace:FindFirstChild("Wormholes")
                            if wormholes then
                                local one = wormholes:FindFirstChild("One")
                                local two = wormholes:FindFirstChild("Two")
                                
                                if one and two and hrp then
                                    if portalTimer == 0 then
                                        hrp.CFrame = one.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = two.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Wormhole Ability + Slap Aura + Portal Teleport Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if wormholeReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(wormholeReceiverLoop)
                wormholeReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

                if char then

                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)

        autoCherryReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then

                local cloneTimer = 0
                
                while autoCherryReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        cloneTimer = cloneTimer + 0.5
                        if cloneTimer >= 0.5 then
                            cloneTimer = 0
                            
                            local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                            if cherryStorage then
                                for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                    if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                        local cloneRemote = model:FindFirstChild("clone_remote")
                                        if cloneRemote then
                                            pcall(function()
                                                cloneRemote:FireServer()
                                            end)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura + Ability + Cherry Clone Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if cherryReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(cherryReceiverLoop)
                cherryReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoCherryHelper = false
local cherryHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("CherryHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Cherry's Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoCherryHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoCherryHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if cherryHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(cherryHelperLoop)
                cherryHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            cherryHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoCherryHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                        if cherryStorage then
                            for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                    local tool = model:FindFirstChild("Cherry")
                                    if tool then
                                        local glove = tool:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                        if glove and glove:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                            hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Cherry Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if cherryHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(cherryHelperLoop)
                cherryHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoBoosterReceiver = false
local boosterReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("BoosterReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoBoosterReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoBoosterReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if boosterReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(boosterReceiverLoop)
                boosterReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            boosterReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoBoosterReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if boosterReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(boosterReceiverLoop)
                boosterReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "BONK",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoBonkReceiver = false
local bonkReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("BonkReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoBonkReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoBonkReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if bonkReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(bonkReceiverLoop)
                bonkReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            bonkReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoBonkReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local bonk = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BONK")
                        if bonk then
                            bonk:FireServer(-0.2956634000001941)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + BONK Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if bonkReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(bonkReceiverLoop)
                bonkReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoBonkHelper = false
local bonkHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("BonkHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoBonkHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoBonkHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if bonkHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(bonkHelperLoop)
                bonkHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            bonkHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoBonkHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if bonkHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(bonkHelperLoop)
                bonkHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- CLOUD TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Cloud",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-4 Quest (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character
        
        local hasCloudGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud"
        local hasEntered = character and character:FindFirstChild("entered")
        local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        
        if not hasCloudGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
            local errorMsg = ""
            if not hasCloudGlove then
                errorMsg = "Equip Cloud Glove"
            elseif not hasEntered then
                errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
            elseif not hasSafespot then
                errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
            end
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = errorMsg,
                Duration = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        if safespot then
            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
            if base then
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                    
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Teleported",
                        Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                        Duration = 2
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("3 Quest")

_G.SetSpeedCloud = 0.5

Tab:AddSlider("CloudSpeedSlider", {
    Title = "Set Speed Cloud",
    Min = 0.1,
    Max = 1.2,
    Default = 0.5,
    Rounding = 0.1,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.SetSpeedCloud = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle("CloudSpeedToggle", {
    Title = "Auto Set Cloud Speed",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.CloudSpeed = Value

        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" then
            while _G.CloudSpeed and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" do
                for i, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name:match(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity") then
                        v.BodyVelocity.Velocity = v.BodyVelocity.Velocity * _G.SetSpeedCloud
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.10)
            end
        elseif _G.CloudSpeed == true then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Cloud",
                Duration = 5
            })
            wait(0.05)
        end
    end
})

end

    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,

        autoSoulReceiver = Value

            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")

                })
                autoSoulReceiver = false
                return
            end

                task.cancel(soulReceiverLoop)
                soulReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            soulReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoSoulReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")

                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer(false)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local soulRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Events")
                        if soulRemote then
                            local soul = soulRemote:FindFirstChild("soul")
                            if soul then
                                soul:FireServer("charge")
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do

                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                            task.wait(1)

                                hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)

                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local busModel = workspace:FindFirstChild("BusModel")
                        if busModel and busModel:IsA("MeshPart") then
                            hrp.CFrame = busModel.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        else
                            local found = false
                            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if obj:IsA("MeshPart") and obj.Name == "BusModel" then
                                    hrp.CFrame = obj.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    found = true
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Bus Teleport Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if busHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(busHelperLoop)
                busHelperLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Spawn Bus (Normal)",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bus" then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").busmoment:FireServer()
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Bus",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Spawn Bus (Fast + Kicks)",
    Callback = function()
        while true do
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").busmoment:FireServer()
            wait()
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- PHASE TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Phase",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoPhaseReceiver = false
local phaseReceiverLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("PhaseReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoPhaseReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoPhaseReceiver = false
                return
            end
            
            if phaseReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(phaseReceiverLoop)
                phaseReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            phaseReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local abilityTimer = 0
                
                while autoPhaseReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                        if abilityTimer >= 14 then
                            abilityTimer = 0
                            local phaseA = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseA")
                            if phaseA then
                                phaseA:FireServer()
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local phaseH = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseH")
                        if phaseH then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        phaseH:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Phase Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if phaseReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(phaseReceiverLoop)
                phaseReceiverLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoPhaseHelper = false
local phaseHelperLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("PhaseHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoPhaseHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                autoPhaseHelper = false
                return
            end
            
            if phaseHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(phaseHelperLoop)
                phaseHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            phaseHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoPhaseHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Ability + Teleport To All Islands (Takes 112 Seconds)",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Phase" and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            local function phaseTo(position)
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(122, 255, 3)
                task.wait(0.1)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").PhaseA:FireServer()
                task.wait(0.1)
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(position)
                task.wait(14)
            end

            phaseTo(Vector3.new(236, -16, -6))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new())
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(4, -5, -223))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(-216, -5, -6))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(-401, 51, -16))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(256, 34, 194))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(4, -5, 215))
            phaseTo(Vector3.new(-125, -5, 122))
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Phase Glove/Use In Arena",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- ============================================================
-- BOMB TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Bomb",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-3 Quest")

Tab:AddToggle("BombTasks", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Bomb" then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Bomb Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Create Safespot first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = true
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        task.wait(1)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(1)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local bombThrow = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BombThrow")
                        if bombThrow then
                            bombThrow:FireServer("Ebutton")
                        end
                        task.wait(1)
                        
                        local bombFound = false
                        for i = 1, 30 do
                            if not getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop then break end
                            
                            for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                if v.Name and string.find(v.Name, "_bømb") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = v.CFrame
                                    bombFound = true
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            
                            if bombFound then
                                break
                            else
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(1)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        if humanoid then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Bomb Tasks",
                Content = "Started! Teleporting to Safespot + Using Bomb",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Throw Bomb/Explode Bomb",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bomb" then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BombThrow:FireServer("Ebutton")
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Bomb",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end

        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BubbleThrow:FireServer()
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle("BubbleAbility", {
    Title = "Auto Use Bubble's Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop = true
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop do
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BubbleThrow:FireServer()
                    task.wait(10)
                end
            end)
        else
            getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Bubble Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bubble" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.BubbleHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Bubble",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end

do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Shard",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3-4-5 Quest (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")
Tab:AddSection("Helper")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

local shardCloneLoop = false

Tab:AddToggle("ShardAbility", {
    Title = "Auto Use Shard's Glove Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            shardCloneLoop = true
            
            spawn(function()
                while shardCloneLoop do
                    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                    
                    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Shard" then
                        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Events.Shards:FireServer()
                        else
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Not Entered",
                                Content = "You need to enter the arena first!",
                                Duration = 3
                            })
                            wait(1)
                        end
                    else
                        Fluent:Notify({
                            Title = "Wrong Glove",
                            Content = "You need Shard glove equipped!",
                            Duration = 3
                        })
                        wait(1)
                    end
                    
                    wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
        else
            shardCloneLoop = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Shard Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        while true do
            local players = game:GetService("Players")
            local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

            for _, player in ipairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                local character = player.Character
                if character then
                    local leftArm = character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
                    if leftArm then
                        replicatedStorage.ShardHIT:FireServer(leftArm)
                    end
                end
            end

            wait(0.5)
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- MOON TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Moon",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local moonToggle = false
local moonGloveLoop = nil
local moonSlapLoop = nil
local moonRagdollLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("MoonReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Ragdoll + Auto Equip/Unequip Glove + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        moonToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while moonToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            moonRagdollLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not moonToggle then return end
                pcall(function()
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                        game.ReplicatedStorage.SelfKnockback:FireServer({
                            ["Force"] = 0,
                            ["Direction"] = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0)
                        })
                    end
                end)
            end)
            
            moonGloveLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not moonToggle then return end
                pcall(function()
                    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                    local character = player.Character
                    
                    if backpack and character then
                        local moonTool = backpack:FindFirstChild("Moon") or character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                        if moonTool then
                            local currentlyEquipped = character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                            if currentlyEquipped then
                                moonTool.Parent = backpack
                            else
                                moonTool.Parent = character
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while moonToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local celestialHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CelestialHit")
                        if celestialHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        celestialHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Moon",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ragdoll + Equip/Unequip + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            if moonRagdollLoop then
                moonRagdollLoop:Disconnect()
                moonRagdollLoop = nil
            end
            if moonGloveLoop then
                moonGloveLoop:Disconnect()
                moonGloveLoop = nil
            end
            moonToggle = false
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

Tab:AddToggle("MoonHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- CHAIN TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Chain",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local chainToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle("ChainReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        chainToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while chainToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Chain",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
