Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Place Tycoon To Safe Spot",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Tycoon" then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            if not hrp then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Character not found!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return
            end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
            task.wait(1)

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(17884, -24, -3539)
            task.wait(1)

            local args = {
                [1] = CFrame.new(17893.552734375, -26.257728576660156, -3535.35888671875, 
                0.00862560048699379, 3.3499091500743816e-08, -0.9999628067016602, 
                8.43312697451637e-10, 1, 3.350761090814558e-08, 
                0.9999628067016602, -1.1323045834288337e-09, 0.00862560048699379)
            }

            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GeneralAbility"):FireServer(unpack(args))
            task.wait(1)

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = "Tycoon placed at safe spot!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Tycoon Glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- 🗿 TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "🗿",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local moaiToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle("MoaiReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        moaiToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while moaiToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local args = {
                                        [1] = base.CFrame
                                    }
                                    generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(14)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "🗿",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

Tab:AddToggle("MoaiHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

        task.spawn(function()
            local players = game:GetService("Players")
            local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local localPlayer = players.LocalPlayer

            while true do
                pcall(function()
                    for _, player in ipairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if player ~= localPlayer then
                            local character = player.Character
                            if character then
                                local leftArm = character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
                                if leftArm then
                                    replicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(leftArm)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

-- ============================================================
-- VOODOO TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Voodoo",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1-2 Quest")

local voodooRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle("VoodooAutoSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(AutoSlapVoodoo)
        voodooRunning = AutoSlapVoodoo
        if not voodooRunning then return end

        task.spawn(function()
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

            local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
                local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
                if #playerList > 1 then
                    local randomPlayer = nil
                    repeat
                        randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                    until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                    local targetChar = randomPlayer.Character
                    if targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        local hrp = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = targetChar.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            local function fireGeneralHitForAllPlayers()
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or 
                                          player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                          player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
                        if targetPart then
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            local count = 0
            while voodooRunning and count < 750 do
                if LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" then
                    teleportToRandomPlayer()
                    fireGeneralHitForAllPlayers()
                    count = count + 1
                    task.wait(0.5)
                else
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Voodoo Glove",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    break
                end
            end
        end)
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("3 Quest")

local voodooAbilityToggle = false
local voodooAbilityLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle("VoodooAbility", {
    Title = "Voodoo Spam Ability Without CD",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        voodooAbilityToggle = state
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if voodooAbilityToggle then
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" then
                voodooAbilityLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while voodooAbilityToggle and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" do
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                        task.wait(3.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                voodooAbilityToggle = false
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Voodoo Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        else
            if voodooAbilityLoop then
                task.cancel(voodooAbilityLoop)
                voodooAbilityLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

end

-- ROB TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "rob",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Create Null Portal (Need Bob And Rob Gloves)",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        
        if not hrp then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Character not found!",
                Duration = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new()
        task.wait(0.5)

        local robClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("rob") and workspace.Lobby.rob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
        if robClick then
            fireclickdetector(robClick)
        end
        task.wait(0.5)
        
        local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
        if robRemote then
            robRemote:FireServer()
        end
        task.wait(0.5)

        local bobClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("bob") and workspace.Lobby.bob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
        if bobClick then
            fireclickdetector(bobClick)
        end
        task.wait(0.5)
        
        local bobRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("bob")
        if bobRemote then
            bobRemote:FireServer()
        end

        Fluent:Notify({
            Title = "Done",
            Content = "Null Portal sequence completed!",
            Duration = 3
        })
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("2 Quest")

local Walkspeed = 20
local KeepWalkspeed = false

Tab:AddSlider("RobWalkspeed", {
    Title = "WalkSpeed",
    Min = 20,
    Max = 1000,
    Default = 20,
    Rounding = 1,
    Callback = function(Value)
        Walkspeed = Value
        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if char then
            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                humanoid.WalkSpeed = Value
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddInput("RobWalkspeedInput", {
    Title = "WalkSpeed",
    Default = "20",
    Placeholder = "Enter walkspeed",
    Callback = function(Value)
        local num = tonumber(Value)
        if num then
            Walkspeed = num
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = num
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle("RobWalkspeedAuto", {
    Title = "Walkspeed Set Auto",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        KeepWalkspeed = Value
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while KeepWalkspeed do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid and humanoid.WalkSpeed ~= Walkspeed then
                                humanoid.WalkSpeed = Walkspeed
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait()
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("3 Quest")

local AutoAbsorb = false

Tab:AddToggle("RobAbsorb", {
    Title = "Auto Absorb People",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoAbsorb = Value
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if AutoAbsorb then
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value:lower() == "rob" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoAbsorb do
                        pcall(function()
                            local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
                            local target = nil
                            local attempts = 0
                            
                            while not target and attempts < 20 do
                                attempts = attempts + 1
                                local randomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
                                if randomPlayer ~= player and randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    target = randomPlayer
                                end
                            end

                            if target then
                                local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                local playerHRP = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                
                                if targetHRP and playerHRP then
                                    playerHRP.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 0, 2)
                                end

                                local ability = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Ability")
                                if ability then
                                    ability:FireServer()
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(1)
                    end
                end)
            else
                AutoAbsorb = false
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Rob Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

local autoRobLoop = false

Tab:AddToggle("RobTransform", {
    Title = "Auto Rob Transformation",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoRobLoop = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoRobLoop do
                    pcall(function()
                        local robObject = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby")
                        if robObject then
                            robObject = robObject:FindFirstChild("rob")
                            if robObject and robObject:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                fireclickdetector(robObject.ClickDetector)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
                        if robRemote then
                            robRemote:FireServer()
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(17)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- FIREWORK TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Firework",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local autoFireworkReceiver = false
local fireworkReceiverLoop = nil
local fireworkSlapAuraConnection = nil
local fireworkAbilityConnection = nil
local fireworkFireworkConnection = nil
local fireworkJumpTimer = 0
local fireworkAbilityTimer = 0
local fireworkSlapTimer = 0
local fireworkFireworkTimer = 0

Tab:AddToggle("FireworkReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Receiver (Safespot + Ability + Firework + Jump + Slap Aura)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoFireworkReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            fireworkJumpTimer = 0
            fireworkAbilityTimer = 0
            fireworkSlapTimer = 0
            fireworkFireworkTimer = 0
            
            if fireworkReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(fireworkReceiverLoop)
                fireworkReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            fireworkReceiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local jumpTimer = 0
                
                while autoFireworkReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then return end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base and base:IsA("BasePart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        jumpTimer = jumpTimer + 0.01
                        if jumpTimer >= 4 then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                            end
                            jumpTimer = 0
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.01)
                end
            end)
            
            if fireworkFireworkConnection then
                fireworkFireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkFireworkConnection = nil
            end
            
            fireworkFireworkConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoFireworkReceiver then 
                    fireworkFireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                    fireworkFireworkConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                fireworkFireworkTimer = fireworkFireworkTimer + deltaTime
                if fireworkFireworkTimer >= 1 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then return end
                        
                        local playerName = player.Name
                        local fireworkPart = workspace:FindFirstChild("Firework_" .. playerName)
                        if fireworkPart and fireworkPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                            hrp.CFrame = fireworkPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                        end
                    end)
                    fireworkFireworkTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            if fireworkAbilityConnection then
                fireworkAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkAbilityConnection = nil
            end
            
            fireworkAbilityConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoFireworkReceiver then 
                    fireworkAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
                    fireworkAbilityConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                fireworkAbilityTimer = fireworkAbilityTimer + deltaTime
                if fireworkAbilityTimer >= 3 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                    end)
                    fireworkAbilityTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            if fireworkSlapAuraConnection then
                fireworkSlapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkSlapAuraConnection = nil
            end
            
            fireworkSlapAuraConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoFireworkReceiver then 
                    fireworkSlapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    fireworkSlapAuraConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                fireworkSlapTimer = fireworkSlapTimer + deltaTime
                if fireworkSlapTimer >= 3 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if not generalHit then return end
                        
                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                            if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if targetPart then
                                    generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    fireworkSlapTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Enabled! Safespot at 0.01s, Firework at 1s, others at 3s.",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if fireworkReceiverLoop then
                task.cancel(fireworkReceiverLoop)
                fireworkReceiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            if fireworkFireworkConnection then
                fireworkFireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkFireworkConnection = nil
            end
            
            if fireworkAbilityConnection then
                fireworkAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkAbilityConnection = nil
            end
            
            if fireworkSlapAuraConnection then
                fireworkSlapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkSlapAuraConnection = nil
            end
            
            fireworkJumpTimer = 0
            fireworkAbilityTimer = 0
            fireworkSlapTimer = 0
            fireworkFireworkTimer = 0
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

local autoFireworkHelper = false
local fireworkHelperLoop = nil
local fireworkHelperJumpTimer = 0

Tab:AddToggle("FireworkHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Helper (Safespot + Firework + Jump + Die on Ragdoll + Auto Re-enter)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoFireworkHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            fireworkHelperJumpTimer = 0
            
            if fireworkHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(fireworkHelperLoop)
                fireworkHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            fireworkHelperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoFireworkHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then 
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return 
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then 
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return 
                        end
                        
                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        
                        for _, part in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(part.Name, "Firework") then
                                hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        
                        fireworkHelperJumpTimer = fireworkHelperJumpTimer + 0.5
                        if fireworkHelperJumpTimer >= 4 then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                            end
                            fireworkHelperJumpTimer = 0
                        end
                        
                        local entered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if entered == nil then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Health = 0
                                    task.wait(2)
                                    
                                    local newChar = player.Character
                                    if newChar then
                                        local newHrp = newChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if newHrp then
                                            newHrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                            task.wait(0.5)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Enabled! Teleporting to Safespot, Firework, Jumping & monitoring ragdoll.",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
        else
            if fireworkHelperLoop then
                task.cancel(fireworkHelperLoop)
                fireworkHelperLoop = nil
            end
            
            fireworkHelperJumpTimer = 0
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- GLOVEL TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Glovel",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local glovelToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle("GlovelReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        glovelToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while glovelToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local glovelFunc = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GlovelFunc")
                        if glovelFunc then
                            glovelFunc:InvokeServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local head = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                                    if head then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(head, true)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Glovel",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

Tab:AddToggle("GlovelHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

-- ============================================================
-- RUN TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Run",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quests (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1-2 Quests")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Closest Player",
    Callback = function()
        local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        local localChar = LocalPlayer.Character
        local localHRP = localChar and localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        
        if not localHRP then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Your character not found!",
                Duration = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        local closestPlayer = nil
        local closestDistance = math.huge
        local closestPos = nil
        
        for _, player in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                local character = player.Character
                local hrp = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    local distance = (hrp.Position - localHRP.Position).Magnitude
                    if distance < closestDistance then
                        closestDistance = distance
                        closestPlayer = player
                        closestPos = hrp.Position
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        if closestPlayer and closestPos then
            localHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(closestPos)
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleported",
                Content = "Teleported to " .. closestPlayer.Name .. " (" .. math.floor(closestDistance) .. " studs away)",
                Duration = 2
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No other players found!",
                Duration = 2
            })
        end
    end
})

local positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
local secondsValue = 7

Tab:AddInput("RunPosition", {
    Title = "Put Position (x, y, z)",
    Default = "0, 0, 0",
    Placeholder = "0, 0, 0",
    Callback = function(Value)
        local parts = {}
        for part in string.gmatch(Value, "([^,]+)") do
            table.insert(parts, tonumber(part))
        end
        
        if #parts >= 3 and parts[1] and parts[2] and parts[3] then
            positionValue = Vector3.new(parts[1], parts[2], parts[3])
        else
            positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddInput("RunSeconds", {
    Title = "Repeat Ability Seconds Delay",
    Default = "7",
    Placeholder = "7",
    Callback = function(Value)
        local num = tonumber(Value)
        if num and num > 0 then
            secondsValue = num
        else
            secondsValue = 7
        end
    end
})

local autoRunEnabled = false

Tab:AddToggle("RunAuto", {
    Title = "Auto Use Run Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoRunEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoRunEnabled do
                    pcall(function()
                        local args = {
                            [1] = positionValue
                        }
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(secondsValue)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- PLANK TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Plank",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quests (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quests")

_G.AutoPlank = false

Tab:AddToggle("PlankAuto", {
    Title = "Auto Use Plank On Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoPlank = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while _G.AutoPlank do
                    pcall(function()
                        local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
                        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local targetPlayers = {}
                        
                        for _, player in ipairs(players) do
                            if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                local hrp = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    table.insert(targetPlayers, {
                                        player = player,
                                        position = hrp.Position
                                    })
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        if #targetPlayers > 0 then
                            local randomTarget = targetPlayers[math.random(1, #targetPlayers)]
                            
                            local args = {
                                [1] = "OutOfBody",
                                [2] = {
                                    ["mousebehavior"] = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default,
                                    ["ismoving"] = false,
                                    ["dir"] = Vector3.new(
                                        randomTarget.position.X,
                                        randomTarget.position.Y,
                                        randomTarget.position.Z
                                    )
                                }
                            }
                            
                            local blink = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Blink")
                            if blink then
                                blink:FireServer(unpack(args))
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

-- EGGLER TAB

do

})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3-4 Quest")
Tab:AddSection("Receiver")

local egglerToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle("EgglerReceiver", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use E and R Abilities + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        egglerToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while egglerToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local events = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Events")
                        if events then
                            local egglerR = events:FindFirstChild("EgglerRAbility")
                            if egglerR then
                                egglerR:FireServer()
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Eggler",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + E/R Abilities + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("Helper")

Tab:AddToggle("EgglerHelper", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end

-- CAR KEYS TAB
-- ============================================================
do
local Tab = Window:AddTab({
    Title = "Car Keys",
    Icon = ""
})

Tab:AddSection("1-2-3 Quests (SOON REWORK)")
Tab:AddSection("|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||")

Tab:AddSection("1 Quest")

local carKeysToggle = false
local upgradeLoop = nil

local attributeFrames = {
    "UtilityAttributeFrame",
    "ArmorAttributeFrame",
    "ReverseAttributeFrame",
    "SteerAngleAttributeFrame",
    "AccelerationAttributeFrame",
    "MaxSpeedAttributeFrame",
    "KnockbackAttributeFrame"
}

Tab:AddToggle("CarKeysUpgrade", {
    Title = "Auto Upgrade All Stats",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        carKeysToggle = Value
        if carKeysToggle then
            upgradeLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while carKeysToggle do
                    for _, attr in ipairs(attributeFrames) do
                        local args = { attr }
                        local carKeysUpgrade = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CarKeysUpgrade")
                        if carKeysUpgrade then
                            carKeysUpgrade:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        else
            if upgradeLoop then
                task.cancel(upgradeLoop)
                upgradeLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddSection("2-3 Quest")

Tab:AddButton({
    Title = "Car Keys Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Car Keys" then
            task.spawn(function()
                local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local Players = game:GetService("Players")
                local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

                while true do
                    pcall(function()
                        for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if player ~= LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                                local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")
                                if rightArm then
                                    ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(rightArm)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Car Keys",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

end

                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end

local ownedBadges = {}

local function fetchOwnedBadges()
    ownedBadges = {}
    
    local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
    if not playerData then return false end
    
    local playerFolder = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
    if not playerFolder then return false end
    
    local unlockedBadges = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("UnlockedBadges")
    if not unlockedBadges then return false end
    
    if unlockedBadges:IsA("StringValue") then
        local badgeIdsString = unlockedBadges.Value
        if badgeIdsString and badgeIdsString ~= "" then
            local trimmed = badgeIdsString:sub(2, -2)
            for id in string.gmatch(trimmed, "[^,]+") do
                local cleanId = id:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                ownedBadges[cleanId] = true
            end
        end
        return true
    end
    return false
end

local WebhookSettings = {
    WebhookURL = "",
    SendInterval = "No time",
    LoggedObjects = {},
    SlapsThreshold = 0,
    NullShardsThreshold = 0,
    Enabled = false,
    PingType = "No Pings",
    UserID = "",
    RoleID = "",
    LastSlapsValue = 0,
    LastNullShardsValue = 0,
    TrackedSlaps = false,
    TrackedNullShards = false,
    SlapsStartValue = 0,
    NullShardsStartValue = 0,
    IsSlapsTracking = false,
    IsNullShardsTracking = false,
    ObjectLogged = {},
    SlapsLogged = false,
    NullShardsLogged = false,
    SlappleLogged = {},
    GoldenSlappleLogged = false,
    LastBadgeCheck = {},
    BadgeLogSent = false,
}

function WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
    local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
    if playerData then
        local userData = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
        if userData then
            local nullShards = userData:FindFirstChild("NullShards")
            if nullShards then
                return nullShards.Value
            end
        end
    end
    return 0
end

local function getPingPrefix()
    if WebhookSettings.PingType == "No Pings" then
        return ""
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@User Ping" and WebhookSettings.UserID ~= "" then
        return "<@" .. WebhookSettings.UserID .. "> "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Role Ping" and WebhookSettings.RoleID ~= "" then
        return "<@&" .. WebhookSettings.RoleID .. "> "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Everyone Ping" then
        return "@everyone "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Here Ping" then
        return "@here "
    end
    return ""
end

local function sendWebhookMessage(content)
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.WebhookURL == "" then return end
    
    local ping = getPingPrefix()
    local fullContent = ping .. content
    
    local payload = {content = fullContent or "No message provided"}
    local jsonData = HttpService:JSONEncode(payload)
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        if syn and syn.request then
            return syn.request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                Body = jsonData
            })
        elseif http_request then
            return http_request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                Body = jsonData
            })
        elseif request then
            return request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                Body = jsonData
            })
        else
            warn("No request method available for webhook!")
            return nil, "No request method available"
        end
    end)
    
    if not success then
        warn("Failed to send webhook: " .. tostring(response))
    end
end

local function getBadgeName(badgeId)
    for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
        if badge.id == badgeId then
            return badge.name
        end
    end
    return "Unknown Badge"
end

    Default = "",
    Placeholder = "Enter webhook URL here",
    Callback = function(Value)
        WebhookSettings.WebhookURL = Value
    end

    Title = "Send Interval",
    Values = {"No time", "30 Seconds", "1 Minute", "10 Minutes", "30 Minutes", "1 Hour", "5 Hours", "10 Hours", "1 Day"},
    Default = 1,
    Callback = function(Value)
        WebhookSettings.SendInterval = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddDropdown("ChooseObjectsSpawnsToLog", {
    Title = "Choose Objects Spawns To Log",
    Values = {"Jet Orb", "Phase Orb", "Glitch Orb", "Siphon Orb", "MATERIALIZE Orb", "Slapple", "Golden Slapple", "Toolbox"},
    Default = {},
    Multi = true,
    Callback = function(Values)
        WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects = Values
        WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
        WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
        for _, obj in pairs(Values) do
            if obj == "Slapple" then
                WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
            elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
            else
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddDropdown("SlapsThreshold", {
    Title = "Slaps Threshold",
    Values = {"100+ Slaps", "1000+ Slaps", "10000+ Slaps", "100000+ Slaps", "1000000+ Slaps", "Custom Slaps Amount"},
    Default = 2,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value == "Custom Slaps Amount" then
            WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = 0
        else
            local num = tonumber(Value:match("(%d+)")) or 0
            WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = num
            WebhookSettings.TrackedSlaps = false
            WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
        end
    end
})

        WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle("EnableWebhookLogging", {
    Title = "Enable Webhook Logging",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        if value then
            WebhookSettings.Enabled = true
            WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
            WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
            WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue
            WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking = true
            WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking = true
            WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.BadgeLogSent = false
            WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck = {}
            
            pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
            for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
                WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
            end
            
            for _, obj in pairs(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects) do
                if obj == "Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
                elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                else
                    WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
                end
            end
            sendWebhookMessage("✅ Webhook logging **STARTED**!")
        else
            sendWebhookMessage("🛑 Webhook logging **STOPPED**!")
            WebhookSettings.Enabled = false
        end
    end
})

-- ============================================================
-- TRACKING FUNCTIONS
-- ============================================================

local function checkObjectSpawns()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end
    
    local objectsToCheck = {
        ["Jet Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("JetOrb"),
        ["Phase Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("PhaseOrb"),
        ["Glitch Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("GlitchOrb"),
        ["Siphon Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("SiphonOrb"),
        ["MATERIALIZE Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("MATERIALIZEOrb"),
        ["Toolbox"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("Toolbox"),
    }
    
    for name, object in pairs(objectsToCheck) do
        if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, name) then
            if object and not WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] then
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = true
                
                local placeName = "Unknown"
                pcall(function()
                    local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                    if info and info.Name then
                        placeName = info.Name
                    end
                end)
                
                local message = string.format(
                    "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** %s\n\n**Name:** %s\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                    name, name, object.Name, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                )
                sendWebhookMessage(message)
            elseif not object then
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = false
            end
        end
    end
    
    if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Slapple") then
        local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
        if slapplesFolder then
            local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
            if island5 then
                local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                if slapples then
                    for _, model in ipairs(slapples:GetChildren()) do
                        if model:IsA("Model") then
                            local gloveMesh = model:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                            if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency
                                local modelName = model.Name
                                
                                if not WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] then
                                    if transparency == 0 then
                                        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = true
                                        
                                        local placeName = "Unknown"
                                        pcall(function()
                                            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                            if info and info.Name then
                                                placeName = info.Name
                                            end
                                        end)
                                        
                                        local message = string.format(
                                            "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Slapple\n\n**Name:** Slapple\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                            modelName, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                        )
                                        sendWebhookMessage(message)
                                    end
                                elseif transparency == 1 then
                                    WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = nil
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Golden Slapple") then
        local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
        if slapplesFolder then
            local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
            if island5 then
                local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                if slapples then
                    local goldenSlapple = slapples:FindFirstChild("GoldenSlapple")
                    if goldenSlapple and goldenSlapple:IsA("Model") then
                        local gloveMesh = goldenSlapple:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                            local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency
                            
                            if transparency == 0 and not WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged then
                                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = true
                                
                                local placeName = "Unknown"
                                pcall(function()
                                    local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                    if info and info.Name then
                                        placeName = info.Name
                                    end
                                end)
                                
                                local message = string.format(
                                    "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Golden Slapple\n\n**Name:** Golden Slapple\n**Real Name:** GoldenSlapple\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                    placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                )
                                sendWebhookMessage(message)
                            elseif transparency == 1 then
                                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

local function checkSlaps()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking then return end
    
    local currentSlaps = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
    local previousSlaps = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue
    
    if currentSlaps >= WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold and currentSlaps > previousSlaps then
        WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = currentSlaps
        local earnedSlaps = currentSlaps - WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue
        
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**Slaps Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Slaps\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Slaps:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
            WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue, currentSlaps, earnedSlaps, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
        )
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
        WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = currentSlaps
    end
end

local function checkNullShards()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking then return end
    
    local currentNullShards = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
    local previousNullShards = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue
    
    if currentNullShards >= WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold and currentNullShards > previousNullShards then
        WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = currentNullShards
        local earnedNullShards = currentNullShards - WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue
        
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**Null Shards Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Null Shards\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Null Shards:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue, currentNullShards, earnedNullShards, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
        )
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
        WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = currentNullShards
    end
end

local function checkBadges()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end
    
    local success = pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
    if not success then return end
    
    local newBadges = {}
    for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
        if not WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] then
            table.insert(newBadges, badgeId)
            WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
        end
    end
    
    if #newBadges > 0 then
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        local newBadgeNames = {}
        for _, id in pairs(newBadges) do
            for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
                if badge.id == id then
                    table.insert(newBadgeNames, badge.name .. " (`" .. id .. "`)")
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        
        local ownedList = {}
        for id, _ in pairs(WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck) do
            table.insert(ownedList, id)
        end
        
        local missingList = {}
        for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
            if badge.category == "GloveRewarding" and not ownedBadges[badge.id] then
                table.insert(missingList, badge.id)
            end
        end
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**🎉 NEW BADGE(S) UNLOCKED!**\n\n" ..
            "**Badge(s):**\n%s\n\n" ..
            "**Place Name:** %s\n" ..
            "**Place ID:** %s\n" ..
            "**JobID:** %s\n\n" ..
            "**Total Badges Unlocked:** %s\n" ..
            "**Missing Glove Badges:** %s",
            table.concat(newBadgeNames, "\n"),
            placeName,
            game.PlaceId,
            game.JobId,
            #ownedList > 0 and #ownedList .. " badges" or "None",
            #missingList > 0 and #missingList .. " badges" or "None"
        )
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
    end
end

local function startWebhookLoop()
    while true do
        if WebhookSettings.Enabled then
            pcall(checkObjectSpawns)
            pcall(checkSlaps)
            pcall(checkNullShards)
            pcall(checkBadges)
        end
        
        local waitTime = 1
        if WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Seconds" then 
            waitTime = 30
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Minute" then 
            waitTime = 60
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Minutes" then 
            waitTime = 600
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Minutes" then 
            waitTime = 1800
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Hour" then 
            waitTime = 3600
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "5 Hours" then 
            waitTime = 18000
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Hours" then 
            waitTime = 36000
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Day" then 
            waitTime = 86400
        end
        
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end

task.spawn(startWebhookLoop)
end
